Oct 30, 2016

I created a method to GET the middle X percent, and it is configurable by changing
the two params <a> and <b> :

http://localhost:5000/helpers/stats/1/bounds/<a>,<b>/

==EXAMPLE==

This is the result of this API, which get the middle 50 percent:

http://localhost:5000/helpers/stats/1/bounds/25,25/
